  <h2 class="date-header">Wednesday, June 20, 2018</h2>
  
       
 
  <!-- Begin post -->
   <div class="post"><a name="4725260915701723083"></a>
   
    
    <h3 class="post-title">
<BlogItemTitle><span class="PostTitle">
<a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2018/06/granny-wolf-bbq-central-park-mall.html">
Granny Wolf BBQ, Central Park Mall, Chippendale Sydney</a></span>    </h3>

    <div class="post-body">
 
      <div>
<div style="float:right;padding:4px;">
      <img alt="Basting chuan skewers on the barbecue at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/884/28006733667_818e57db4a_o.jpg" title="Basting chuan skewers on the barbecue at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<b><br />
</b> <b>Bulgogi beef? Cumin lamb? Chicken gizzards?</b> It's a choose-your-own skewer adventure at <b>Granny Wolf BBQ</b>, newly arrived at Central Park, taking over the former site of Lang Suan Thai Street Food. The fit out is flash and modern, a beacon of backlit neon cleverly incorporating a wolf's open jaw.<br />
<br />
The concept is simple. Grab a tray and browse the self-serve chilled bain marie of assorted skewers. These are chuan, small street food skewers that originated in Xinjiang, China but have now spread in popularity across the country. The use of cumin as a seasoning for many of the skewers is a reference to their Chinese Islamic Uyghur origins. But here too you'll find other influences, including Korean bulgogi sauce and Taiwanese sausages.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Self-serve chuan skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1768/42875393511_e8284a66f9_o.jpg" title="Self-serve chuan skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Self-serve skewer station</span></i><br />
<br />
Everything is clearly labelled in both English and Chinese. It's a mixed bag of lamb, chicken, pork and beef. Vegetarian choices are limited to shiitake mushrooms and corn cobs although you can add orders of fries, wedges, sweet potato fries and salads (cucumber and garlic, celery and yuba or shredded kelp).<br />
<br />
<img alt="Taiwanese sausage, Cantonese sausage and cheese fish tofu skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/899/42875399311_c8d98562ba_o.jpg" title="Taiwanese sausage, Cantonese sausage and cheese fish tofu skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Taiwanese sausage </i>$5 each</span><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Cantonese sausage and cheese fish tofu skewers </i>$2.50 each</span><br />
<br />
<img alt="Bulgogi beef brisket skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/899/29003560978_f59178e5ac_o.jpg" title="Bulgogi beef brisket skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Bulgogi beef brisket skewers&nbsp;</i><span style="color: #990000;">$2.50 each</span><br />
<br />
<img alt="Pickled pepper beef brisket skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1752/28006741607_78edd7504a_o.jpg" title="Pickled pepper beef brisket skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Pickled pepper beef brisket skewers&nbsp;</i><span style="color: #990000;">$2.50 each</span><br />
<br />
<img alt="Cumin chicken heart skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1809/42875397241_7046d8cf15_o.jpg" title="Cumin chicken heart skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Cumin chicken heart skewers&nbsp;</i><span style="color: #990000;">$2.50 each</span><br />
<br />
<img alt="Teriyaki beef tongue skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/879/28006738917_c1af1c126d_o.jpg" title="Teriyaki beef tongue skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Teriyaki beef tongue skewers&nbsp;</i><span style="color: #990000;">$2.50 each</span><br />
<br />
<img alt="Seasoning skewers on the bbq at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1801/28006735557_ff2d95049c_o.jpg" title="Seasoning skewers on the bbq at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Seasoning skewers on the bbq</i></span><br />
<br />
Once you're ready, take them to the counter and add any other menu options. The skewers are cooked on the barbecue grill in the front window. Warning: they do take about 5-10 minutes to cook so don't arriving starving.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Marinated pig trotters with steamed rice at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1821/29003563318_564558139c_o.jpg" title="Marinated pig trotters with steamed rice at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Granny Wolf Supreme Meal combo&nbsp;</i><span style="color: #990000;">$15.50</span><br />
<span style="color: #990000;">Marinated pig trotters with steamed rice, 3 x $2.50 skewers and homemade plum juice</span><br />
<br />
The <b>Supreme Meal Combo</b> is probably one of the best value deals, presuming you're ok with eating pork skin. It's a massive serve of rice - perfect for eating with your skewers - topped with two chunks of<b> pig trotter</b> (tasty but more pork skin and fat than meat, as expected).<br />
<br />
The <b>seaweed salad </b>and <b>celery yuba salad</b> are also welcomed, providing a welcome hit of acidity when you tuck into the skewers (they're coming. Eventually).<br />
<br />
<img alt="Spicy bulgogi beef brisket; chicken giblet; and spice pepper with cumin lamb skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1764/29003564078_63ff71d82e_o.jpg" title="Spicy bulgogi beef brisket; chicken giblet; and spice pepper with cumin lamb skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Spicy bulgogi beef brisket; chicken giblet; and spice pepper with cumin lamb skewers </i><span style="color: #990000;">$2.50 each</span><br />
<br />
In addition to the pouch of homemade plum juice, you get to choose any three $2.50 skewers. I go with <b>spicy bulgogi beef</b>, <b>chicken giblets </b>and <b>cumin lamb</b>. You'll be asked how spicy you'll like your skewers when they're cooked. I go with super spicy and let me tell you, they're not kidding around.<br />
<br />
The meat is cooked to well done, so expect some satisfying chewiness to it. It's not dry though. I enjoy the chicken giblets the most, but that's because I've always loved their crunch.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Self-serve seasonings at the counter at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/899/29003562128_df6d66079a_o.jpg" title="Self-serve seasonings at the counter at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Self-serve seasonings at the counter</i></span><br />
<br />
Don't forget to make use of the self-serving seasonings at the counter when you pick up your order either.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Braised pork belly with rice at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1757/29003566478_2dbe284e98_o.jpg" title="Braised pork belly with rice at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Braised pork belly with rice </i><span style="color: #990000;">$10.50</span><br />
<br />
On my second visit, I hightail it to the<b> braised pork belly with rice</b>. It's listed as a side but is more of a main meal, accompanied with celery yuba salad, half a boiled egg and a mountain of plain rice. You could easily share these between two (I did). And there's a lot of braised pork belly in here too (more meat than fat which I personally find disappointing).<br />
<br />
<img alt="Cantonese sausage; spice pepper with cumin lamb; pickled pepper beef brisket; and spicy bulgogi pork belly skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1734/29003570268_41c494d42a_o.jpg" title="Cantonese sausage; spice pepper with cumin lamb; pickled pepper beef brisket; and spicy bulgogi pork belly skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Cantonese sausage; spice pepper with cumin lamb; pickled pepper beef brisket; and spicy bulgogi pork belly skewers </i><span style="color: #990000;">$2.50 each</span><br />
<br />
We hit up more skewers, including the<b> Cantonese sausage</b>; spice pepper with <b>cumin lamb</b>; <b>pickled pepper beef brisket</b>; and <b>spicy bulgogi pork belly</b>. The pork belly is the star with its caramelised fatty bits.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Crispy chicken skin at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1724/29003567658_47736aaefa_o.jpg" title="Crispy chicken skin at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Crispy chicken skin </i><span style="color: #990000;">$5.50</span><br />
<br />
The <b>crispy chicken skin</b> isn't as overall crispy as we'd hoped. There are some crunchy pieces but others are a little soggier, with that squelch of unrendered chicken fat. It's a huge portion though, and recommended for sharing between 2-3 people unless you really want to give your arteries a workout.<br />
<br />
<img alt="New Orleans grilled chicken bones at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/884/29003569528_388dfaaaa7_o.jpg" title="New Orleans grilled chicken bones at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">New Orleans grilled chicken bones&nbsp;</i><span style="color: #990000;">$5</span><br />
<br />
The unexpected highlight is this: <b>New Orleans grilled chicken bones</b>. They come in a pyrex tray in the chilled bain marie, a selection of carcass cast-offs that run from ribs to necks to pelvic bones. $5 might sound ridiculous but I reckon you get more meat from this than two skewers.<br />
<br />
Because the bones take a little longer to cook, there's a smokier flavour too, plus the carnivorous satisfaction of crunching down all the burnt bits of bone and cleaning every last juicy skerrick of flesh off every bone. I'd definitely eat this again.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Cantonese sausage; spice pepper with cumin lamb; pickled pepper beef brisket; and spicy bulgogi pork belly skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1768/29003568568_5ea1123690_o.jpg" title="Cantonese sausage; spice pepper with cumin lamb; pickled pepper beef brisket; and spicy bulgogi pork belly skewers at Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Skewer party</i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1755/29003565498_e34d33f3f8_o.jpg" title="Granny Wolf BBQ in Central Park Mall Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<br />

  <h2 class="date-header">Monday, June 11, 2018</h2>
  
       
 
  <!-- Begin post -->
   <div class="post"><a name="3899698425853914004"></a>
   
    
    <h3 class="post-title">
<BlogItemTitle><span class="PostTitle">
<a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2018/06/lakemba-ramadan-food-festival-2018.html">
Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018</a></span>    </h3>

    <div class="post-body">
 
      <div>
<div style="float:right;padding:4px;">
      <img alt="Street stall at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1738/40905222610_d78ee5c79d_o.jpg" title="Street stall at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<br />
Four nights. That's how many nights you have left to visit one of <b>Sydney's most vibrant and family-friendly night food markets</b>. The Ramadan Food Festival in Lakemba is a community iftar, the breaking of the day's Ramadan fast at dusk.<br />
<br />
The markets kick off at 5pm, as the sun sets, with festivities running until 4am. It's a delicious event, and incredibly cheap. Rug up, bring a pocketful of cash and travel around the world via Lakemba.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Ful medames fava beans at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1738/40905220030_af16a5c54d_o.jpg" title="Ful medames fava beans at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Ful medames fava beans, a traditional dish to eat for iftar</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Meats on the grill at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1721/42666367062_fc3d321c45_o.jpg" title="Meats on the grill at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Grilled meats on the barbecue</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Boiled corn cobs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1756/42666367982_afdf817150_o.jpg" title="Boiled corn cobs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Boiled corn</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Saj bread cooking at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1759/40905217790_04a481d187_o.jpg" title="Saj bread cooking at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Cooking saj flat bread</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Saj bread with Nutella at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1724/27846397247_e3e627cc2a_o.jpg" title="Saj bread with Nutella at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Spreading Nutella onto saj flat bread</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Flipping paratha roti at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1735/41997204674_94f4644424_o.jpg" title="Flipping paratha roti at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Flipping paratha dough</span></i><br />
<br class="Apple-interchange-newline" /> <img alt="Adding egg and oinon to paratha roti to make martabak at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1746/27846416307_75e4528491_o.jpg" title="Adding egg and oinon to paratha roti to make martabak at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Adding beaten egg and onion to paratha dough</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Martabak telur roti paratha at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1738/27846414287_08279f7066_o.jpg" title="Martabak telur roti paratha at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<div><i><span style="color: #990000;">Filled paratha folded into martabak</span></i></div><br />
<img alt="Cooked beans at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1741/27846401957_67c1f5ceb0_o.jpg" title="Cooked beans at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Cooked chickpeas, fava beans and lupin beans</i></span><br />
<br />
<img alt="Camel burgers cooking over charcoal at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1729/27846422547_76e60e23e1_o.jpg" title="Camel burgers cooking over charcoal at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Camel burgers being cooking over charcoal</span></i><br />
<br />
The queue for camel burgers is always hectic.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Carrot juice stall at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1752/27846405347_68a5ecdc64_o.jpg" title="Carrot juice stall at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Fresh carrot juice stall</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Chicken doner kebab at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1752/40905229230_c54d193b42_o.jpg" title="Chicken doner kebab at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Carving chicken doner kebab</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Brisket by 2 Smokin' Arabs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1742/40905214570_76ae886587_o.jpg" title="Brisket by 2 Smokin' Arabs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>2 Smokin' Arabs</i></span><br />
<br />
It's worth checking out the pop-up by <b>2 Smokin' Arabs</b>, a BBQ competition team who have temporarily taken up residence in a former newsagency on Haldon Street.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Carved brisket by 2 Smokin' Arabs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1756/27846394537_ac87c1f535_o.jpg" title="Carved brisket by 2 Smokin' Arabs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Carved beef brisket</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Brisket box and hot wings by 2 Smokin' Arabs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1726/27846424837_97ed123c03_o.jpg" title="Brisket box and hot wings by 2 Smokin' Arabs at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Brisket box </i>$20&nbsp;</span><br />
<i><span style="color: #990000;">Hot wings&nbsp;</span></i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Chicken tikka skewers on the charcoal bbq at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1753/27846408747_7bd9fe51eb_o.jpg" title="Chicken tikka skewers on the charcoal bbq at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<div><i style="color: #990000;">Chicken tikka skewers cooked over charcoal</i></div><br />
<img alt="Chicken tikka skewers on charcoal at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1738/41997202954_655a8cb7c0_o.jpg" title="Chicken tikka skewers on charcoal at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Caramelised chicken tikka skewers</i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Grilled corn at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1726/27846399557_3a63969eca_o.jpg" title="Grilled corn at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Barbecued corn skewers grilled over charcoal</i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Knafeh dessert served in kaak sesame bread at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1757/27846420407_dd1e81ebf9_o.jpg" title="Knafeh dessert served in kaak sesame bread at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Knafeh served in kaak</i><br />
<br />
For dessert, it's hard to go past a serve of <b>knafeh</b>. At this stall you can get your knafeh served in <b>kaak</b> bread...<br />
<br />
<img alt="Knafeh at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1729/41815588305_38f4a528cf_o.jpg" title="Knafeh at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<div><i style="color: #990000;">Knafeh</i></div><div><br />
</div><div>but we had ours served straight onto a plate. It's a textural party of warm cheese, crunchy semolina and sweet syrup drizzled across the top.<br />
<br />
</div><img alt="Palestinian knafeh at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1738/41815585055_7736a4a433_o.jpg" title="Palestinian knafeh at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Palestinian knafeh</i><br />
<br />
The <b>Palestinian knafeh</b> comes with saffron-tinted kataifi pastry and a sprinkle of pistachio nuts.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Palestinian knafeh slice at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1753/41815581395_3dddf1655e_o.jpg" title="Palestinian knafeh slice at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Oozy cheesy Palestinian knafeh</i><br />
<br />
The Palestinian knafeh is much cheesier in flavour with a more noticeable stretchiness. Guaranteed fun when you're hovering on the footpath with a plastic fork!<br />
<br />
<img alt="Serving up Palestinian knafeh at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1746/27846418217_b5a43578d8_o.jpg" title="Serving up Palestinian knafeh at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Palestinian knafeh for one</i><br />
<br />
<img alt="Kaak Lebanese bread with cheese grilled over charcoal at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1741/40905225340_7db1b36da5_o.jpg" title="Kaak Lebanese bread with cheese grilled over charcoal at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Kaak bread with cheese grilling over charcoal</i><br />
<br />
Still hungry? Do what we did. Get a grilled cheese sandwich, Lebanese-style. Kaak bread is stuffed with a haloumi-like cheese and toasted over charcoal.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Melted cheese inside kaak bread at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1728/40905232430_bfb2c0ae97_o.jpg" title="Melted cheese inside kaak bread at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Melted cheese inside kaak</i><br />
<br class="Apple-interchange-newline" /> Oozing hot cheese. Nutty toasted sesame seeds. And crisp and toasty bread that's slightly smoky from the charcoal.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Turkish coffee brewed in hot sand at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1742/27846411097_63318e5c2d_o.jpg" title="Turkish coffee brewed in hot sand at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Turkish coffee&nbsp;</i><br />
<br />
And if you still want to party on, get a Turkish coffee brewed in hot sand. You'll be going all night!<br />
<br />
<img alt="Pouring Turkish coffee brewed in hot sand at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1745/40905234800_0284aef426_o.jpg" title="Pouring Turkish coffee brewed in hot sand at Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2018 on Haldon Street" width="500" /><br />
<br />
<iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="400" src="https://www.google.com/maps/embed?pb=!1m18!1m12!1m3!1d52971.57851916599!2d151.0435971802768!3d-33.92251118064134!2m3!1f0!2f0!3f0!3m2!1i1024!2i768!4f13.1!3m3!1m2!1s0x6b12bbc5cb3f5a71%3A0x463b6525552f2f8!2sHaldon+St%2C+Lakemba+NSW+2195!5e0!3m2!1sen!2sau!4v1528696803062" style="border: 0;" width="500"></iframe><br />
<div><span style="color: #660000;"><br />
</span></div><span style="color: #660000;"><br />
</span> <b><span style="color: #660000;">The Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival runs every night from 5pm (sunset) through to 4am.&nbsp;Crowds tend to peak 8pm-10pm.&nbsp;The final night will be Thursday 14 June 2018.</span></b><br />
<span style="color: #660000;"><br />
</span> <span style="color: #660000;">Food stalls are set up along Haldon Street near Lakemba rail station, between The Boulevarde and Gillies Street. Some nights you will also find stalls along Railway Parade.</span><br />
<span style="color: #660000;"><br />
</span> <span style="color: #660000;">Due to the popularity of this event, street parking tends to fill quickly so take public transport if possible.</span><br />
<i><br />
</i> <i>See more pics from the&nbsp;</i><a href="https://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2016/07/ramadan-food-festival-lakemba.html">Lakemba Ramadan Food Festival 2016</a>
    </div>
 
    </div>

  <h2 class="date-header">Wednesday, June 06, 2018</h2>
  
       
 
  <!-- Begin post -->
   <div class="post"><a name="3700778516501332237"></a>
   
    
    <h3 class="post-title">
<BlogItemTitle><span class="PostTitle">
<a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2018/06/black-bear-bbq-blacktown.html">
Black Bear BBQ, Blacktown</a></span>    </h3>

    <div class="post-body">
 
      <div>
<div style="float:right;padding:4px;">
      <img alt="Ben Huppatz  holding bbq brisket at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1727/40667968750_3477e6c911_o.jpg" title="Ben Huppatz holding bbq brisket at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<br />
<b>Low and slow. </b>That's the ethos behind<b> Black Bear BBQ</b>, serving up Texan-style woodsmoked barbecue. You'll find them in the back streets of Blacktown, feeding a non-stop queue of hungry tradies and office workers. There's nothing fancy here. Just massive serves of meat served up in takeaway cardboard boxes, and that's exactly the way the locals like it.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Barbecue at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/898/40667975880_f5f3103c2e_o.jpg" title="Barbecue at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<br />
You'll know you've arrived when you spot the picnic tables out the front and the giant light bulb letters spelling BBQ.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Black Bear BBQ menu in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1741/42476317991_4cc7e0ccac_o.jpg" title="Black Bear BBQ menu in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Black Bear BBQ menu</i></span><br />
<br />
It's one helluva meat fest on the menu. Vegetarians aren't really catered for here, unless you're happy with slaw, pickles and a handful of crisps.<br />
<br />
Order at the counter (yes, they have EFTPOS) and enjoy the spectacle of your meat being carved up before your eyes.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Barbecue pork ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1724/40667967380_3e75770ddb_o.jpg" title="Barbecue pork ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Barbecue pork ribs</i></span><br />
<br />
Barbecue porks ribs are cut through with ease...<br />
<br />
<img alt="Beef brisket at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1735/40667965470_84b2d4d482_o.jpg" title="Beef brisket at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Beef brisket</i><br />
<br />
but it's the huge slab of beef brisket, covered in a deep black bark, that's guaranteed to get your mouth watering.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Beef short ribs, beef brisket, links, pork belly and pork ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1760/41754056904_d04e6d72eb_o.jpg" title="Beef short ribs, beef brisket, links, pork belly and pork ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Lunch for three</i><br />
<br />
The meat boxes range in price from $15 to $25, each bolstered with crisps, pickles and a rainbow slaw of cabbage, carrot, celery and corn. The drinks fridge includes plenty of American favourites like Dr Pepper and Canada Dry.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Pork ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1760/41754059234_34e66f7c90_o.jpg" title="Pork ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Half rack pork ribs </i><span style="color: #990000;">$35</span><br />
<br class="Apple-interchange-newline" /> We feast on all the meats, starting with a half rack of <b>pork ribs</b>. They're impressively tender (only a smidge dry at the thicker end of the rib) with its sweet glaze enhanced by a generous dousing of barbecue sauce.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Sausage link, beef brisket and pork belly at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1739/40667971300_8a59a627c1_o.jpg" title="Sausage link, beef brisket and pork belly at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<span style="color: #990000;"><i>Hungry Bear Box&nbsp;</i>$25</span><br />
<span style="color: #990000;">Links, brisket and pork belly</span><br />
<br />
The <b>Hungry Bear Box</b> yields a triple threat of <b>links, brisket and pork belly</b>. The <b>brisket</b> has a lush layer of fat although it's not quite as smoky as we expect, even with the visible smoke ring. There's a good ribbon of fat running through the <b>pork belly</b>, cooked to a caramelised juiciness.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Sausage link stuffed with cheese at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/894/41754061024_9381cfa874_o.jpg" title="Sausage link stuffed with cheese at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Sausage link with cheese</i><br />
<br />
The<b> sausage link </b>is a real highlight through, the springy smoky sausage stuffed with cubes of cheese. I'd definitely order this again.<br />
<br class="Apple-interchange-newline" /> <img alt="Beef short ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/882/40667973550_fd3964a2b3_o.jpg" title="Beef short ribs at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<i style="color: #990000;">Beef short rib box</i><span style="color: #990000;">&nbsp;$25</span><br />
<div><span style="color: #990000;"><br />
</span></div>The <b>beef short rib box </b>usually comes with only one rib but because there are only two small end ribs left in the tray, we score both. Win! It's a fatty reward, just the way we like it, the beef cooked long enough so the fat has rendered throughout. <a href="http://www.chocolatesuze.com/">Suze</a> reports that it was heavily smoky in flavour on her last visit. Today there's a subtler imparting of smoke to the meat.<br />
<br />
Here's the bad news. They're only open weekdays although they do open most Friday nights - I hear the queues are hectic so be prepared to wait. Otherwise you can do as we did and take a day off work for a trip out west. They're open from 6am for breakfast (brisket and egg roll, anyone?) with lunch (and the meat boxes) starting at 11am.<br />
<br />
<img alt="Outdoor seating at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" height="700" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/890/41754063244_bb54fbcfa1_o.jpg" title="Outdoor seating at Black Bear BBQ in Blacktown Sydney" width="500" /><br />
<br />
<iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="400" src="https://www.google.com/maps/embed?pb=!1m18!1m12!1m3!1d212105.27449547983!2d150.9416988231089!3d-33.83437328100472!2m3!1f0!2f0!3f0!3m2!1i1024!2i768!4f13.1!3m3!1m2!1s0x6b1298e1ab332273%3A0xe6f7b3f5c7c8fb81!2sBlack+Bear+BBQ!5e0!3m2!1sen!2sau!4v1528212275772" style="border: 0;" width="500"></iframe><br />
<a href="https://www.zomato.com/sydney/black-bear-bbq-blacktown" target="_blank" title="View Menu, Reviews, Photos &amp; Information about Black Bear BBQ, Blacktown and other Restaurants in Sydney"><img alt="Black Bear BBQ Menu, Reviews, Photos, Location and Info - Zomato" src="https://www.zomato.com/logo/17744983/minilogo" style="border: none; height: 15px; padding: 0px; width: 104px;" /></a><br />
<br />
<a href="http://blackbearbbq.com.au/"><b>Black Bear BBQ</b></a><br />
<span style="color: #660000;">11/27 Forge Street, Blacktown, Sydney</span><br />
<span style="color: #660000;">Tel: +61 (02) 8605 3953</span><br />
<span style="color: #660000;"><br />
</span> <span style="color: #660000;">Opening hours</span><br />

<span style="color: #660000;">Friday 6am-2pm, <a href="https://www.facebook.com/blackbearhire/">most nights</a> 6.30pm until sold out&nbsp;</span><br />

<a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com" title="Go back to the GrabYourFork home page">GRAB YOUR FORK</a> is Helen's gastronomic journey around Sydney and the world. She is a freelance food writer with a love of cheap eats, offal and fried chicken. Her work has been published in <a href=" http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2015/05/toyama-black-ramen-firefly-squid-and.html#good_food " title="Cover story on Cheap Eats for Good Food">Good Food</a> and <a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2012/04/cheap-eats-2012.html" title="Cover story on Cheap Eats and other restaurant reviews for Time Out Sydney">Time Out Sydney</a>. She was Cheap Eats editor for <a href=" http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2011/08/eating-and-drinking-sydney-guide.html" title="About my editor role for 2012 Eating and Drinking Sydney">2012 Eating and Drinking Sydney</a> and has contributed to <a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2010/09/2011-foodies-guide-to-sydney.html" title="About The Foodies' Guide to Sydney">The Foodies' Guide to Sydney</a>, the <a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2010/07/food-lovers-guide-to-chinatown-and.html" title="About the Food Lovers Guide to Chinatown & Haymarket">Food Lovers Guide to Chinatown</a> and <a href="http://grabyourfork.blogspot.com/2011/05/voracious-best-new-australian-food.html" target="_blank" title="Read my essay in Voracious">Voracious: The Best New Australian Food Writing</a>.
